<li id="cite_note-48"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-48">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation journal">Mohr, Peter J.; Newell, David B.; Taylor, Barry N. <a class="external text" href="http://codata.org/blog/2015/08/04/codata-recommended-values-of-the-fundamental-physical-constants-2014/" rel="nofollow">CODATA recommended values of the fundamental physical constants: 2014 – Summary</a>. Zenodo. 2015 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2017-04-10</span>]</span>. <a class="external text" href="https://dx.doi.org/10.5281%2Fzenodo.22827" rel="nofollow"><span title="数位物件识别号">doi:10.5281/zenodo.22827</span></a>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20160201122217/http://codata.org/blog/2015/08/04/codata-recommended-values-of-the-fundamental-physical-constants-2014/" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2016-02-01）. <q>Because of the good progress made in both experiment and theory since the 31 December 2010 closing date of the 2010 CODATA adjustment, the uncertainties of the 2014 recommended values of <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r58896141">.mw-parser-output .serif{font-family:Times,serif}</style><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml mvar" style="font-style:italic;margin-left:2px;margin-right:2px;">h</span></span>, <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml mvar" style="font-style:italic;margin-left:2px;margin-right:2px;">e</span></span>, <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml mvar" style="font-style:italic;margin-left:2px;margin-right:2px;">k</span></span> and <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml"><i>N</i><sub>A</sub></span></span> are already at the level required for the adoption of the revised SI by the 26th CGPM in the fall of 2018. The formal road map to redefinition includes a special CODATA adjustment of the fundamental constants with a closing date for new data of 1 July 2017 in order to determine the exact numerical values of <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml mvar" style="font-style:italic;margin-left:2px;margin-right:2px;">h</span></span>, <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml mvar" style="font-style:italic;margin-left:2px;margin-right:2px;">e</span></span>, <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml mvar" style="font-style:italic;margin-left:2px;margin-right:2px;">k</span></span> and <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml"><i>N</i><sub>A</sub></span></span> that will be used to define the New SI. A second CODATA adjustment with a closing date of 1 July 2018 will be carried out so that a complete set of recommended values consistent with the New SI will be available when it is formally adopted by the 26th CGPM.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E5%9B%BD%E9%99%85%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E5%88%B6&amp;rft.atitle=CODATA+recommended+values+of+the+fundamental+physical+constants%3A+2014+%E2%80%93+Summary&amp;rft.au=Newell%2C+David+B.&amp;rft.au=Taylor%2C+Barry+N.&amp;rft.aufirst=Peter+J.&amp;rft.aulast=Mohr&amp;rft.date=2015&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=Zenodo&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fcodata.org%2Fblog%2F2015%2F08%2F04%2Fcodata-recommended-values-of-the-fundamental-physical-constants-2014%2F&amp;rft_id=info%3Adoi%2F10.5281%2Fzenodo.22827&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-NIST330-49"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-NIST330_49-0"><sup><b>46.0</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-NIST330_49-1"><sup><b>46.1</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-NIST330_49-2"><sup><b>46.2</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-NIST330_49-3"><sup><b>46.3</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-NIST330_49-4"><sup><b>46.4</b></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Thompson, Ambler; Taylor, Barry N. <a class="external text" href="http://physics.nist.gov/Pubs/SP330/sp330.pdf" rel="nofollow">The International System of Units (SI) (Special publication 330)</a> <span style="font-size:85%;">(PDF)</span>. Gaithersburg, MD: National Institute of Standards and Technology. 2008 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2008-06-18</span>]</span>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20181225010952/https://physics.nist.gov/Pubs/SP330/sp330.pdf" rel="nofollow">存档</a> <span style="font-size:85%;">(PDF)</span>于2018-12-25）.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E5%9B%BD%E9%99%85%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E5%88%B6&amp;rft.au=Taylor%2C+Barry+N.&amp;rft.aufirst=Ambler&amp;rft.aulast=Thompson&amp;rft.btitle=The+International+System+of+Units+%28SI%29+%28Special+publication+330%29&amp;rft.date=2008&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.place=Gaithersburg%2C+MD&amp;rft.pub=National+Institute+of+Standards+and+Technology&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fphysics.nist.gov%2FPubs%2FSP330%2Fsp330.pdf&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
